The ISO 8601 standard for date and time representation specifies a format that includes the following elements:
- Date: YYYY-MM-DD, where YYYY represents the four-digit year, MM represents the two-digit month (01-12), and DD represents the two-digit day (01-31).
- Time: HH:MM:SS, where HH represents the two-digit hour (00-23), MM represents the two-digit minute (00-59), and SS represents the two-digit second (00-59).
- Timezone: Z for UTC (Coordinated Universal Time) or ±HH:MM for a specific offset from UTC.

The ISO 8601 standard specifies a format for representing date and time information. The format follows the pattern: YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS.sssZ, where:
- YYYY represents the four-digit year.
- MM represents the two-digit month (01-12).
- DD represents the two-digit day of the month (01-31).
- T is a separator indicating the start of the time portion.
- HH represents the two-digit hour of the day in 24-hour format (00-23).
- MM represents the two-digit minute (00-59).
- SS represents the two-digit second (00-59
